		<span style="color: #75715e">//creating color array</span>
		
		<span style="color: #a6e22e">p</span><span style="color: #f8f8f2">.</span><span style="color: #a6e22e">colorMode</span><span style="color: #f8f8f2">(</span><span style="color: #a6e22e">p</span><span style="color: #f8f8f2">.</span><span style="color: #a6e22e">RGB</span><span style="color: #f8f8f2">);</span>

	<span style="color: #f8f8f2">};</span>
	<span style="color: #a6e22e">p</span><span style="color: #f8f8f2">.</span><span style="color: #a6e22e">mouseClicked</span> <span style="color: #f92672">=</span> <span style="color: #66d9ef">function</span><span style="color: #f8f8f2">()</span> <span style="color: #f8f8f2">{</span>

	<span style="color: #f8f8f2">};</span>
